<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
My fault for going the next day after a big rain storm. Basically slid down the path to beach on my bottom. It's basically a steep dirt path down to beach from parking lot. There's another way towards the north but need to walk a longer way 15-20mins. Fell the second step down and basically just get up and slide, get up and slide. Don't go after big rain. The beach is nice and off leash for dogs so lots of dogs. That's the main reason we go, for the dogs.</Text>

Lied about sauce. Why?
I called in to order, and asked "Do you have creamy garlic sauce?" The man answered "Yes," so I ordered a pizza. Picked up my pizza and drove home. As I ate my pizza, I thought it didn't taste garlicky. I lifted the cheese and looked under, thinking maybe they forgot the sauce? But the crust was moist so there was some kind of sauce. So I checked my receipt, and it said Ranch Sauce.
What was the point of lying about this? Did the man taking my order think I wouldn't notice? If he had been honest, I would have gotten a pizza elsewhere. By lying he got my $20 today, but lost any future business from me.
Today is my birthday and I had a great day, and wanted to finish it with a great dinner. Sad that I chose Pizza Factory of Twain Harte.</review>

< text>
This used to be an inn back in the day and was the place to go. It hosted celebrities and had individual cottages with fireplaces and kitchenettes. The main building held a dining room and bar.
It was turned into a rehabilitation center for head injured patients until that was disbanded.
Now it hosts businesses in the small cottages and Bass Hill house is right above it.< /text>

< Text>
The manager, Michael should be fired!

I have been an AT&T customer since September 2014, and on 2/20/2017, I came into the store to change my plan. Sabrina greeted me and offered assistance to me, she is very helpful and friendly! After revising my plan, I asked her how much it would cost to change my cellphone number, and she said it would be at no cost and so I decided to change my cellphone number.

I reviewed my monthly statement and discovered that I was charged $36 for changing my cellphone number so I commuted back to the store. On 3/3/2017, at approximately 1:50pm, I met with Sabrina again. I explained to her that I had been charged $36 after she had assured me that there would be no cost to changing my cellphone number. She was puzzled, and began to examine my AT&T customer account on her tablet. She located the $36 charge and walked the tablet towards the back of the store where the manager, Michael was stationed. Michael said to Sabrina that the charge was valid and then he instructed her to walk back to me to tell me to call '611' because there was nothing that could be done at the physical store to adjust the $36 charge. Michael is a liar! Or perhaps he was too lazy at the time to help Sabrina correct this problem because she had misled me by offering me false information during my 2/20/2017 visit.

Sabrina walked back to me and instructed me to call '611'. I was disappointed because she didn't even apologize for inconveniencing me. It was because of her misinformation that I was now charged $36 and now she expected me to do all the work to fix it!? Any positive impression I had of Sabrina from 2/20/2017 was now quickly evaporating. I asked her if I could call '611' inside the store because the AT&T operator might ask me for Sabrina's testimony, or perhaps she might be able to assist me some other way.

Suddenly Michael yelled at me from across the room! He realized that his lazy resolve, to have me dismissed from the store by instructing me to leave and call '611' on my own, was foiled so then he stood up from his station and aggressively stormed on over to me to confront me. He yelled and condescended me, "you need to calm down!" Both Sabrina and I were stunned by Michael's erratic behavior. I hesitated then replied, "did I raise my voice?" Realizing that he had become too trigger-happy too hastily, Michael began to backpedal and responded to my question, "no, you did not raise your voice but I could hear it in your tone-of-voice! If you don't calm down then you will have to leave the store!" I was astonished at Michael's ability to fabricate falsehoods. I calmly explained to Michael that I was going to call '611' in the store and I might ask Sabrina for help. Michael was desperately searching for reasons to warrant his unhinged demeanor but to his dismay, he only discovered embarrassment in himself, and so he retreated back to his station.

While I was waiting in the phone for a live AT&T operator to come to the line, I asked Sabrina for the store business card. She politely complied with my request and then she walked back towards Michael to retrieve a business card to satisfy my request. Michael stonewalled Sabrina, instructing her to halt. Sabrina stood still, while Michael focused on pushing away at the tablet that was still logged onto my AT&T customer account. A few minutes elapsed and then Michael marched on over to me with the tablet in his hand and presented that he had manually adjusted $36 against my account balance. "Now that I've credited your account, you can now get out of my store!" I was shocked and appalled.

I walked towards the front door and before leaving, I said to Michael, "I hope that you enjoy your job while you still have it," and then I exited the store.

This is when things become scary: While I was walking back to my car, Michael exited the store to follow me! Michael yelled, "hey, come back here!" It was apparent that he wanted to quarrel and that he was inviting a physical confrontation. How can AT&T employ this person, let alone making him a manager, Michael is unhinged!<//Text>

<Review>Hi guys, I just wanted to review two of your products I have on my 2005 G35 sedan. (Very positive).
Your nismo style rear lip and nismo style side skirts were a dream to install. It took me 30 minutes or less to swap the side skirts over. They fit better than the OEM ones, using OEM hardware. They also provide more clearance for jacks and jack stands than the OEM ones did. Outstanding.
Installing your rear lip was also surprisingly easy. I used speed nut style hardware that bit into the OEM plastic bumper from underneath with 1/4-20 stainless hardware. No double sided tape needed. The result was a removable, steadily mounted lip with tight body lines thanks to your mold design.
You guys changed my mind about fiberglass products. Your parts do not feel brittle and ready to crack at any moment, they are flexible and sturdy.
I will be back to purchase some carbon fiber products in the near future.< /Review>< Date>

< text>
I love Mongolian bbq and they do the best! You have to fill out a paper if you walk in with what you want, you just go thru and circle what you want as far as type of meat, veggies and how any scoops of the different types of sauces. If you are not sure let them know you want flavor and or if you want it spicy and they are more than happy to help you fill it out. They will hook you up and it is the bomb. The Mongolian bbq is $10.77 out the door, it comes with your choice of chicken fried rice or white rice and a veggie egg roll. Mask is required to enter and they do have plastic up around. They do ask if your ordering any thing else besides Mongolian bbq call the order on ahead of time and pick it up (signs posted). The portions are large and me and my husbands can share and get full!< /text>

<review>I started eating here when this place first opened. The restaurant was clean, the food was good, and the staff was friendly. Most of that hasn't changed.

I visit for the first time in years and am taken aback by how things have deteriorated. Outside the restaurant was swarming with transients, some waiting outside the door to hit people up for money. I'm all for helping people but let the business do business! Inside looked run down.  It looked like they hadn't changed anything from 15 years ago when they opened. Literally nothing.

It took an exceedingly long time to get our drinks and appetizers. When we did, all of our drinks were noticeably and insultingly watered down.

On the positive, the food was still good in spite of the lack of ambiance. The person who helped us was polite and accommodating. Cant beat the cream cheese wontons. I just hope they clean up some issues.</review>< pictures>

THIS RESTAURANT WAS YELLOW CARDED ON 9-18-2018 FOR FILTHY CONDITIONS AND THEY HAD TO THROW OUT THE FOOD!

AND WAS CLOSED DOWN DUE TO COCKROACHES ON FEB 18 2016!

I went into Silver Garden today for lunch and I always check the Sac County Restaurant Inspection Placard posted out by the front door. There's also a mobile app you can get on your phone to instantly check to see if it's a minor offense or something that might want you to think twice!

It stated that Silver Garden had a previous closure. So I kept walking until I could check it out. Here's the link:

emdinspections.saccounty‚Ä¶

I decided to go somewhere else because after you read the report from Feb 2016 regarding cockroaches crawling over food and "severe grease and food build up" it's hard to enjoy your meal.

Truth be told, honestly I've never eaten here but I wanted to have my fellow Yelpers fully informed when they make decisions where to eat and where to spend their hard earned money.

Appetite ruined....< /review>

<Rate>5< /Rate><review>Nothing I like more than a local Mom n Pop family oriented restaurant that serves excellent food! Friendly staff, good service, great food and extremely affordable price.

Been a huge fan of this place for over a decade. They have everything here. Awesome lunch & dinner combos. Chinese Food and Mongolian BBQ. A nice option to pick from.

Let's start with their Mongolian BBQ. I like it hot. Left over eating cold is even better cause it taste better than 15$ a La Bou Salad. For a good sized bowl filled with meat and vegetables, 1.5 scoop of all the dark sauces and 2 full scoops of oil ( combo of sesame and hot.) bowl of  cabbage soup, rice (steamed or fried) and egg rolls comes with it! Cheese wonton with dinner combo. Did I mention they make BEST cream cheese wontons in the world???

Their Chinese food is out of this world. I can't find another place to compare it with. Wor Wonton Soup is super hearty with chicken, beef shrimp loaded with cabbage. A meal within itself. Their Fried Rice and chow mein is un believably tasty. Walnut prawns, is so creamy it melts in your mouth. Chicken wings, cheese wontons, general chicken & triple delight. YUMM! I can't name everything off the menu. But EVERYTHING they make is good!

It's Chinese American Fusion and I am addicted to this place.< /review><pictures>None<//pictures><response>None< /response><gmapID>0x809ad9282e99a27f:0xf3168a13fc67cba1</gmapID></record></dataset><record>
